
Steps:

My strategy has always been to work with the OSI model from bottom to top on communication issues.

1. Was able to get logged into the server.
2. Verify IP ifconfig
3. Look at ARP table
4. Ping Gateway
5. Looked at eth0 config.  One theory is that this is a DHCP IP and not static so the address
   changes thus clients can't get into the system anymore.
6. Traceroute
7. Curl to local host see if anything is on 80 or 443
8. Looked at Netstat to see what ports are listening on the box.  Not seeing any application on 80 or 443.
9. Top to verify processes
10. Looked at message log file to for any error messages.
11. I tried to start the httpd but may not be setup on this box or need to look more into AWS commands and see if there
    is some application services which need started.
